	<script>
 window.dataLayer = window.dataLayer || [];
  function gtag(){dataLayer.push(arguments);}
    var cookieValue = '';
  var name = 'g_c_consent' + "=";
  var decodedCookie = decodeURIComponent(document.cookie);
  var ca = decodedCookie.split(';');
  for(var i = 0; i <ca.length; i++) {
	var c = ca[i];
	while (c.charAt(0) == ' ') {
	  c = c.substring(1);
	}
	if (c.indexOf(name) == 0) {
	  cookieValue = c.substring(name.length, c.length);
	}
  }



if(cookieValue == ''){
	gtag('consent', 'default', {
	  'ad_storage': 'denied',
	  'ad_user_data': 'denied',
	  'ad_personalization': 'denied',
	  'analytics_storage': 'denied',
	  'personalization_storage': 'denied',
	  'functionality_storage': 'denied',
	  'security_storage': 'denied'
	});
	} else if(cookieValue != '-1'){


			gtag('consent', 'default', {
			'ad_storage': 'granted',
			'ad_user_data': 'granted',
			'ad_personalization': 'granted',
			'analytics_storage': 'granted',
			'personalization_storage': 'granted',
			'functionality_storage': 'granted',
			'security_storage': 'granted'
		});
	} else {
	 gtag('consent', 'default', {
		  'ad_storage': 'denied',
		  'ad_user_data': 'denied',
		  'ad_personalization': 'denied',
		  'analytics_storage': 'denied',

		});

<script>
	function gaBuildProductVariant(product)
	{
		let _return = '';
		if(product.version != undefined)
		{
			$.each(product.version, function(i, a){
				_return += (_return == '' ? '' : ', ')+a.value;
			})
		}
		return _return;
	}

</script>
 
<script>
	$.Gomag.bind('Product/Add/To/Cart/After/Listing', function gaProductAddToCartLV4(event, data) {
		if(data.product !== undefined) {
			var gaProduct = false;
			if(typeof(gaProducts) != 'undefined' && gaProducts[data.product.id] != undefined)
			{
				gaProduct = gaProducts[data.product.id];

			}

			if(gaProduct == false)
			{
				gaProduct = {};
				gaProduct.item_id = data.product.id;
				gaProduct.currency = data.product.currency ? (String(data.product.currency).toLowerCase() == 'lei' ? 'RON' : data.product.currency) : 'RON';
				gaProduct.item_name =  data.product.name ;
				gaProduct.item_variant= gaBuildProductVariant(data.product);
				gaProduct.item_brand = data.product.brand;
				gaProduct.item_category = data.product.category;

			}

			gaProduct.price = parseFloat(data.product.price).toFixed(2);
			gaProduct.quantity = data.product.productQuantity;
			gtag("event", "add_to_cart", {
				currency: gaProduct.currency,
				value: parseFloat(gaProduct.price) * parseFloat(gaProduct.quantity),
				items: [
					gaProduct
				]
			});

		}
	})
	$.Gomag.bind('Product/Add/To/Cart/After/Details', function gaProductAddToCartDV4(event, data){

		if(data.product !== undefined){

			var gaProduct = false;
			if(
				typeof(gaProducts) != 'undefined'
				&&
				gaProducts[data.product.id] != undefined
			)
			{
				var gaProduct = gaProducts[data.product.id];
			}

			if(gaProduct == false)
			{
				gaProduct = {};
				gaProduct.item_id = data.product.id;
				gaProduct.currency = data.product.currency ? (String(data.product.currency).toLowerCase() == 'lei' ? 'RON' : data.product.currency) : 'RON';
				gaProduct.item_name =  data.product.name ;
				gaProduct.item_variant= gaBuildProductVariant(data.product);
				gaProduct.item_brand = data.product.brand;
				gaProduct.item_category = data.product.category;

			}

			gaProduct.price = parseFloat(data.product.price).toFixed(2);
			gaProduct.quantity = data.product.productQuantity;


			gtag("event", "add_to_cart", {

	 $.Gomag.bind('Product/Remove/From/Cart', function gaProductRemovedFromCartV4(event, data){
		var envData = $.Gomag.getEnvData();
		var products = envData.products;

		if(data.data.product !== undefined && products[data.data.product] !== undefined){


			var dataProduct = products[data.data.product];


			gaProduct = {};
			gaProduct.item_id = dataProduct.id;

			gaProduct.item_name =   dataProduct.name ;
			gaProduct.currency = dataProduct.currency ? (String(dataProduct.currency).toLowerCase() == 'lei' ? 'RON' : dataProduct.currency) : 'RON';
			gaProduct.item_category = dataProduct.category;
			gaProduct.item_brand = dataProduct.brand;
			gaProduct.price = parseFloat(dataProduct.price).toFixed(2);
			gaProduct.quantity = data.data.quantity;
			gaProduct.item_variant= gaBuildProductVariant(dataProduct);
			gtag("event", "remove_from_cart", {
			  currency: gaProduct.currency,
			  value: parseFloat(gaProduct.price) * parseFloat(gaProduct.quantity),
			  items: [
				gaProduct
			  ]
			});
        }

	});

	 $.Gomag.bind('Cart/Quantity/Update', function gaCartQuantityUpdateV4(event, data){
		var envData = $.Gomag.getEnvData();
		var products = envData.products;
		if(!data.data.finalQuantity || !data.data.initialQuantity)
		{
			return false;
		}
		var dataProduct = products[data.data.product];
		if(dataProduct == undefined)
		{
			return false;
		}

		gaProduct = {};
		gaProduct.item_id = dataProduct.id;
		gaProduct.currency = dataProduct.currency ? (String(dataProduct.currency).toLowerCase() == 'lei' ? 'RON' : dataProduct.currency) : 'RON';
		gaProduct.item_name =  dataProduct.name ;

		gaProduct.item_category = dataProduct.category;
		gaProduct.item_brand = dataProduct.brand;
		gaProduct.price = parseFloat(dataProduct.price).toFixed(2);
		gaProduct.item_variant= gaBuildProductVariant(dataProduct);
		if(parseFloat(data.data.initialQuantity) < parseFloat(data.data.finalQuantity))
		{
			var quantity = parseFloat(data.data.finalQuantity) - parseFloat(data.data.initialQuantity);
			gaProduct.quantity = quantity;

			gtag("event", "add_to_cart", {
			  currency: gaProduct.currency,
			  value: parseFloat(gaProduct.price) * parseFloat(gaProduct.quantity),
			  items: [
				gaProduct
			  ]
			});
		}
		else if(parseFloat(data.data.initialQuantity) > parseFloat(data.data.finalQuantity))
		{
			var quantity = parseFloat(data.data.initialQuantity) - parseFloat(data.data.finalQuantity);
			gaProduct.quantity = quantity;
			gtag("event", "remove_from_cart", {
			  currency: gaProduct.currency,
			  value: parseFloat(gaProduct.price) * parseFloat(gaProduct.quantity),
			  items: [
				gaProduct
			  ]
			});
		}

	});

</script>

<script>
function gaCGBuildProductVariant(product)
	{
		let _return = '';
		if(product.version != undefined)
		{
			$.each(product.version, function(i, a){
				_return += (_return == '' ? '' : ', ')+a.value;
			})
		}
		return _return;
	}

</script>

<script>
	$.Gomag.bind('Product/Add/To/Cart/After/Listing', function gaProductAddToCartLGCV4(event, data){
		if(data.product !== undefined){

			var gaProduct = false;
			if(typeof(gaProducts) != 'undefined' && gaProducts[data.product.id] != undefined)
			{
				gaProduct = gaProducts[data.product.id];

			}

			if(gaProduct == false)
			{
				gaProduct = {};
				gaProduct.item_id = data.product.id;
				gaProduct.currency = data.product.currency ? data.product.currency : 'RON';
				gaProduct.item_name = data.product.sku;
				gaProduct.item_variant= gaCGBuildProductVariant(data.product);
				gaProduct.item_brand = data.product.brand;
				gaProduct.item_category = data.product.category;

			}

			gaProduct.price = parseFloat(data.product.price).toFixed(2);
			gaProduct.quantity = data.product.productQuantity;

			gtag("event", "add_to_cart", {
				send_to: 'gomag',
				currency: gaProduct.currency,
				value: parseFloat(gaProduct.price) * parseFloat(gaProduct.quantity),
				items: [
					gaProduct
				]
			});

        }
	})

	 $.Gomag.bind('Product/Remove/From/Cart', function gaProductRemovedFromCartGCV4(event, data){
		var envData = $.Gomag.getEnvData();
		var products = envData.products;

		if(data.data.product !== undefined && products[data.data.product] !== undefined){


			var dataProduct = products[data.data.product];


			gaProduct = {};
			gaProduct.item_id = dataProduct.id;

			gaProduct.item_name = dataProduct.sku;
			gaProduct.currency = dataProduct.currency;
			gaProduct.item_category = dataProduct.category;
			gaProduct.item_brand = dataProduct.brand;
			gaProduct.price = parseFloat(dataProduct.price).toFixed(2);
			gaProduct.item_variant= gaCGBuildProductVariant(dataProduct);
			gaProduct.quantity = data.data.quantity;
			gtag("event", "remove_from_cart", {
				send_to: 'gomag',
			  currency: gaProduct.currency,
			  value: parseFloat(gaProduct.price) * parseFloat(gaProduct.quantity),
			  items: [
				gaProduct
			  ]
			});
        }

	});

	 $.Gomag.bind('Cart/Quantity/Update', function gaCartQuantityUpdateV4(event, data){
		var envData = $.Gomag.getEnvData();
		var products = envData.products;
		if(!data.data.finalQuantity || !data.data.initialQuantity)
		{
			return false;
		}
		var dataProduct = products[data.data.product];
		if(dataProduct == undefined)
		{
			return false;
		}

		gaProduct = {};
		gaProduct.item_id = dataProduct.id;
		gaProduct.currency = dataProduct.currency ? dataProduct.currency : 'RON';
		gaProduct.item_name = dataProduct.sku;
		gaProduct.item_variant= gaCGBuildProductVariant(dataProduct);
		gaProduct.item_category = dataProduct.category;
		gaProduct.item_brand = dataProduct.brand;
		gaProduct.price = parseFloat(dataProduct.price).toFixed(2);

		if(parseFloat(data.data.initialQuantity) < parseFloat(data.data.finalQuantity))
		{
			var quantity = parseFloat(data.data.finalQuantity) - parseFloat(data.data.initialQuantity);
			gaProduct.quantity = quantity;

			gtag("event", "add_to_cart", {
				send_to: 'gomag',
				currency: gaProduct.currency,
				value: parseFloat(gaProduct.price) * parseFloat(gaProduct.quantity),
				items: [
					gaProduct
				]
			});
		}
		else if(parseFloat(data.data.initialQuantity) > parseFloat(data.data.finalQuantity))
		{
			var quantity = parseFloat(data.data.initialQuantity) - parseFloat(data.data.finalQuantity);
			gaProduct.quantity = quantity;
			gtag("event", "remove_from_cart", {
				send_to: 'gomag',
			  currency: gaProduct.currency,
			  value: parseFloat(gaProduct.price) * parseFloat(gaProduct.quantity),
			  items: [
				gaProduct
			  ]
			});
		}

	});

                const cMinutes = parseInt(popupSettings['countdown']['minutes']);
                seconds = cDays * 3600 * 24 + cHours * 3600 + cMinutes * 60 + parseInt(popupSettings['countdown']['seconds']);
            } else {

                if (popupSettings['countdown']['end_date'] === null || new Date(popupSettings['countdown']['end_date']) <= new Date()) {
                    const countdownEl = document.getElementById('mkt-popup-content-countdown');

                    if (countdownEl) {
                        countdownEl.remove();
                    }
                }

                const endDate = new Date(popupSettings['countdown']['end_date']);
                const currentDate = new Date();

                seconds = Math.abs(endDate - currentDate) / 1000;
            }

            const getCountdownRemainingTime = () => {
                const days = popupSettings['countdown']['display_days'] ? Math.floor(seconds / 24 / 60 / 60) : 0;
                const hoursLeft = Math.floor((seconds) - (days * 86400));
                const hours = popupSettings['countdown']['display_hours'] ? Math.floor(hoursLeft / 3600) : 0;
                const minutesLeft = Math.floor((hoursLeft) - (hours * 3600));
                const minutes = popupSettings['countdown']['display_minutes'] ? Math.floor(minutesLeft / 60) : 0;
                const remainingSeconds = seconds % 60;

                const countdownEl = document.getElementById('mkt-popup-content-countdown');
                const countdownDaysEl1 = document.getElementById('mkt-popup-content-countdown-days-1');
                const countdownDaysEl2 = document.getElementById('mkt-popup-content-countdown-days-2');
                const countdownHoursEl1 = document.getElementById('mkt-popup-content-countdown-hours-1');
                const countdownHoursEl2 = document.getElementById('mkt-popup-content-countdown-hours-2');
                const countdownMinutesEl1 = document.getElementById('mkt-popup-content-countdown-minutes-1');
                const countdownMinutesEl2 = document.getElementById('mkt-popup-content-countdown-minutes-2');
                const countdownSecondsEl1 = document.getElementById('mkt-popup-content-countdown-seconds-1');
                const countdownSecondsEl2 = document.getElementById('mkt-popup-content-countdown-seconds-2');

                if (countdownDaysEl1) {
                    const dDigits = days.toString();

                    countdownDaysEl1.innerHTML = days >= 10 ? dDigits[0] : 0;
                    countdownDaysEl2.innerHTML = days >= 10 ? dDigits[1] : dDigits[0];
                }

                if (countdownHoursEl1) {
                    const hDigits = hours.toString();

                    countdownHoursEl1.innerHTML = hours >= 10 ? hDigits[0] : 0;
                    countdownHoursEl2.innerHTML = hours >= 10 ? hDigits[1] : hDigits[0];
                }

                if (countdownMinutesEl1) {
                    const mDigits = minutes.toString();

                    countdownMinutesEl1.innerHTML = minutes >= 10 ? mDigits[0] : 0;
                    countdownMinutesEl2.innerHTML = minutes >= 10 ? mDigits[1] : mDigits[0];
                }

                if (countdownSecondsEl1) {
                    const sDigits = remainingSeconds.toString();

                    countdownSecondsEl1.innerHTML = remainingSeconds >= 10 ? sDigits[0] : 0;
                    countdownSecondsEl2.innerHTML = remainingSeconds >= 10 ? sDigits[1] : sDigits[0];
                }

                if (seconds <= 0) {
                    clearInterval(countdownTimer);

                    if (popupSettings['countdown']['when_reaching_zero'] === 'show_message') {
                        countdownEl.innerHTML = popupSettings['countdown']['zero_message'];
                    } else {
                        countdownEl.remove();
                    }
                } else {
                    seconds--;
                }
            };

            const countdownTimer = setInterval(getCountdownRemainingTime, 1000);
        } else {
            const countdownEl = document.getElementById('mkt-popup-content-countdown');
            countdownEl && countdownEl.remove();
        }

        // date input

        const checkDateInputValue = (e) => {
            if (parseInt(e.target.value) < 10 && e.target.value.indexOf('0') !== 0) {
                e.target.value = '0' + e.target.value;
            }

            if (parseInt(e.target.value) < e.target.min) {
                e.target.value = e.target.min;
            }

            if (parseInt(e.target.value) > e.target.max) {
                e.target.value = e.target.max;
            }
        }

        let dateErrorEl = null;
        const hasDateInput = popupSettings.form_fields.find(field => field.id === 'date_of_birth' && !popupSettings['date_of_birth']['hide']);

        if (hasDateInput) {
            dateErrorEl = document.getElementById('mkt-content-input-required-dob');
            const dayInputEl = document.getElementById("mkt_popup_birthday_day");
            const yearInputEl = document.getElementById("mkt_popup_birthday_year");
            const monthInputEl = document.getElementById("mkt_popup_birthday_month");

            if (dayInputEl && yearInputEl && monthInputEl) {

                monthInputEl.onkeydown = function (e) {
                    handleChange("mkt_popup_birthday_month", e);

                    if (dateErrorEl && dateErrorEl.style.display === 'block') {
                        dateErrorEl.style.display = 'none';
                    }
                }

                monthInputEl.addEventListener('change', (e) => {
                    checkDateInputValue(e);
                });

                dayInputEl.onkeydown = function (e) {
                    handleChange("mkt_popup_birthday_day", e);

                    if (dateErrorEl && dateErrorEl.style.display === 'block') {
                        dateErrorEl.style.display = 'none';
                    }
                }

                dayInputEl.addEventListener('change', (e) => {
                    checkDateInputValue(e);
                });

                yearInputEl.onkeydown = function (e) {
                    handleChange("mkt_popup_birthday_year", e);

                    if (dateErrorEl && dateErrorEl.style.display === 'block') {
                        dateErrorEl.style.display = 'none';
                    }
                }

                yearInputEl.addEventListener('change', (e) => {
                    checkDateInputValue(e);
                });
            }

            function handleChange(id, e) {
                document.getElementById(id).value.length === 0 && e.key === "Backspace" && document.getElementById(id === "mkt_popup_birthday_month" ? "mkt_popup_birthday_day" : id === "mkt_popup_birthday_year" && "mkt_popup_birthday_month") && document.getElementById(id === "mkt_popup_birthday_month" ? "mkt_popup_birthday_day" : id === "mkt_popup_birthday_year" ? "mkt_popup_birthday_month" : "").focus();

                document.getElementById(id).value.length === document.getElementById(id).maxLength && e.key !== "Backspace" && document.getElementById(id === "mkt_popup_birthday_day" ? "mkt_popup_birthday_month" : id === "mkt_popup_birthday_month" && "mkt_popup_birthday_year") && document.getElementById(id === "mkt_popup_birthday_day" ? "mkt_popup_birthday_month" : id === "mkt_popup_birthday_month" ? "mkt_popup_birthday_year" : "").focus();
            }
        }

        // email input

        const emailInputEl = document.getElementById('mkt_popup_subscriber_email');
        const alreadySubscribedEl = document.getElementById('mkt-content-input-exists-email');
        let emailRequiredEl;

        if (emailInputEl) {
            const emailErrorEl = document.getElementById('mkt-content-input-error-email');
            emailRequiredEl = document.getElementById('mkt-content-input-required-email');

            emailInputEl.addEventListener('input', () => {

                if (alreadySubscribedEl && alreadySubscribedEl.style.display === 'block') {
                    alreadySubscribedEl.style.display = 'none';
                }

                if (emailErrorEl && emailErrorEl.style.display === 'block') {
                    emailErrorEl.style.display = 'none';
                }

                if (emailRequiredEl && emailRequiredEl.style.display === 'block') {
                    emailRequiredEl.style.display = 'none';
                }
            });

            emailInputEl.addEventListener('change', (e) => {
                if (!checkEmailFormat(e.target.value)) {

                    if (emailErrorEl) {
                        emailErrorEl.style.display = 'block';
                    }

                    wrongEmailFormat = true;

                } else {
                    wrongEmailFormat = false;
                }
            });
        }

        // name input

        const nameInputEl = document.getElementById('mkt_popup_subscriber_name');
        let nameErrorEl = null;

        if (nameInputEl) {
            nameErrorEl = document.getElementById('mkt-content-input-required-name');

            nameInputEl.addEventListener('input', () => {

                if (nameErrorEl && nameErrorEl.style.display === 'block') {
                    nameErrorEl.style.display = 'none';
                }
            });

            nameInputEl.addEventListener('change', (e) => {
                if (!e.target.value) {

                    if (nameErrorEl) {
                        nameErrorEl.style.display = 'block';
                    }
                }
            });
        }

        // first name input

        const firstNameInputEl = document.getElementById('mkt_popup_subscriber_first_name');
        let firstNameErrorEl = null;

        if (firstNameInputEl) {
            firstNameErrorEl = document.getElementById('mkt-content-input-required-first_name');

            firstNameInputEl.addEventListener('input', () => {

                if (firstNameErrorEl && firstNameErrorEl.style.display === 'block') {
                    firstNameErrorEl.style.display = 'none';
                }
            });

            firstNameInputEl.addEventListener('change', (e) => {
                if (!e.target.value) {

                    if (firstNameErrorEl) {
                        firstNameErrorEl.style.display = 'block';
                    }
                }
            });
        }

        // last name input

        const lastNameInputEl = document.getElementById('mkt_popup_subscriber_last_name');
        let lastNameErrorEl = null;

        if (lastNameInputEl) {
            lastNameErrorEl = document.getElementById('mkt-content-input-required-last_name');

            lastNameInputEl.addEventListener('input', () => {

                if (lastNameErrorEl && lastNameErrorEl.style.display === 'block') {
                    lastNameErrorEl.style.display = 'none';
                }
            });

            lastNameInputEl.addEventListener('change', (e) => {
                if (!e.target.value) {

                    if (lastNameErrorEl) {
                        lastNameErrorEl.style.display = 'block';
                    }
                }
            });
        }

        // phone input

        const phoneInputEl = document.getElementById('mkt_popup_subscriber_phone');
        let phoneErrorEl = null;

        if (phoneInputEl) {
            phoneErrorEl = document.getElementById('mkt-content-input-required-phone');

            phoneInputEl.addEventListener('input', () => {

                if (phoneErrorEl && phoneErrorEl.style.display === 'block') {
                    phoneErrorEl.style.display = 'none';
                }
            });

            phoneInputEl.addEventListener('change', (e) => {
                if (!e.target.value) {

                    if (phoneErrorEl) {
                        phoneErrorEl.style.display = 'block';
                    }
                }
            });
        }

        // gender select

        const genderInputEl = document.getElementById('mkt_popup_subscriber_gender');

        let genderErrorEl = null;

        if (genderInputEl) {
            genderErrorEl = document.getElementById('mkt-content-input-required-gender');

            genderInputEl.addEventListener('input', () => {

                if (genderErrorEl && genderErrorEl.style.display === 'block') {
                    genderErrorEl.style.display = 'none';
                }
            });

        }

        const getGender = () => {
            const genderSelectEl = document.getElementById('mkt_popup_subscriber_gender');

            return genderSelectEl ? genderSelectEl.value !== '' ? genderSelectEl.value : null : null;
        }

        // privacy policy

        const privacyPolicyEl = document.getElementById('mkt_popup_subscriber_privacy_policy');
        let privacyPolicyErrorEl = null;

        if (privacyPolicyEl) {
            privacyPolicyErrorEl = document.getElementById('mkt-content-input-required-privacy');

            privacyPolicyEl.addEventListener('change', () => {
                if (privacyPolicyErrorEl && privacyPolicyErrorEl.style.display === 'block') {
                    privacyPolicyErrorEl.style.display = 'none';
                }
            });
        }

        const getPrivacyPolicy = () => {
            if (privacyPolicyEl) {
                return privacyPolicyEl.checked;
            }
        }

        // custom inputs

        const customFields = {
            custom_form_field_1: {
                el: null,
                error: null
            },
            custom_form_field_2: {
                el: null,
                error: null
            },
            custom_form_field_3: {
                el: null,
                error: null
            }
        };

        ['custom_form_field_1', 'custom_form_field_2', 'custom_form_field_3'].forEach(id => {
            customFields[id].el = document.getElementById(`mkt_popup_subscriber-${id}`);

			if (popupSettings[id].type === 'checkbox') {
				customFields[id].el = document.getElementById(`mkt_popup_subscriber-${id}-checkboxes`)
            }

            if (customFields[id].el) {
                customFields[id].error = document.getElementById(`mkt-content-input-required-${id}`);

                customFields[id].el.addEventListener('input', () => {

                    if (customFields[id].error && customFields[id].error.style.display === 'block') {
                        customFields[id].error.style.display = 'none';
                    }
                });

                customFields[id].el.addEventListener('change', (e) => {
                    if (!e.target.value) {

                        if (customFields[id].error) {
                            customFields[id].error.style.display = 'block';
                        }
                    }
                });

                customFields[id].el.addEventListener('change', (e) => {
                    if (!e.target.value) {

                        if (customFields[id].error) {
                            customFields[id].error.style.display = 'block';
                        }
                    }
                });

                const optionEls = customFields[id].el.querySelectorAll('span.mkt-content-multiple-select-dropdown-option');

                optionEls.forEach((optionEL, index) => {
                    optionEL.addEventListener('click', (ev) => {

                        let currentSelectedOptions = [];

                        optionEls.forEach((oEl, idx) => {
                            if (oEl.classList.contains('selected')) {
                                currentSelectedOptions.push(popupSettings[`${id}`].options[idx]);
                            } else {
                                currentSelectedOptions = currentSelectedOptions.filter(cso => cso !== popupSettings[`${id}`].options[idx]);
                            }
                        });

                        optionEL.classList.toggle('selected');

                        if (optionEL.classList.contains('selected')) {
                            currentSelectedOptions.push(popupSettings[`${id}`].options[index]);
                        } else {
                            currentSelectedOptions = currentSelectedOptions.filter(cso => cso !== popupSettings[`${id}`].options[index]);
                        }

                        const placeholderEl = document.getElementById(`mkt-content-multiple-select-dropdown-ph-${id}`);

                        if (placeholderEl) {
                            if (currentSelectedOptions.length > 0) {
                                placeholderEl.innerHTML = '';

                                currentSelectedOptions.forEach(option => {
                                    const optionEl = document.createElement('span');
                                    optionEl.classList.add('mkt-content-multiple-select-current-option');
                                    optionEl.innerHTML = option;

                                    placeholderEl.appendChild(optionEl);
                                });

                            } else {
                                placeholderEl.innerHTML = popupSettings[`${id}`].placeholder;
                            }
                        }

                    });
                });

				if (popupSettings[id].type === 'checkbox' && !popupSettings[id]['allow_multiple_choices']) {
					if (popupSettings[id].options && popupSettings[id].options.length > 0) {
						const allFieldCheckboxes =  customFields[id].el.querySelectorAll(`[id^="mkt_popup_subscriber-${id}"]`);

                        if (allFieldCheckboxes) {
                            allFieldCheckboxes.forEach(fC => {
                                fC.addEventListener('change', (event) => {
                                    allFieldCheckboxes.forEach((cEl) => {
                                        cEl.checked = false;
                                    });

									fC.checked = !fC.checked;
                                });
                            });
                        }
                    }
                }

            }
        });

        const getCustomFieldInputValue = field => {
            const fieldEl = document.getElementById(`mkt_popup_subscriber-${field}`);

            if (fieldEl) {
                if (popupSettings[field]['type'] === 'input') {
                    return fieldEl.value ? fieldEl.value : null;
                }

                if (popupSettings[field]['type'] === 'select') {

                    if (popupSettings[field]['allow_multiple_choices']) {
                        return getMultipleSelectValues(fieldEl, field);
                    } else {
                        return fieldEl.value ? fieldEl.value : null;
                    }
                }

                if (popupSettings[field]['type'] === 'checkbox') {
                    return getMultipleCheckboxValues(field);
                }
            }
        }

        const getMultipleSelectValues = (selectEl, id) => {
            let result = '';
            const optionValues = [];

            selectEl.querySelectorAll('span.mkt-content-multiple-select-dropdown-option').forEach((optionEL, idx) => {
                if (optionEL.classList.contains('selected')) {
                    optionValues.push(popupSettings[`${id}`].options[idx]);
                }
            });

            optionValues.forEach((value, index) => {
                result += value;

                if (index < optionValues.length - 1) {
                    result += ', ';
                }
            })

            return result;
        }

        const getMultipleCheckboxValues = (id) => {
            let result = '';
			const checkboxWrapper = document.getElementById(`mkt_popup_subscriber-${id}-checkboxes`);

			if (checkboxWrapper) {
				const checkboxEls = checkboxWrapper.querySelectorAll(`[id^="mkt_popup_subscriber-${id}"]`);

				if (checkboxEls && popupSettings[id].options.length === 0) {
					return checkboxEls[0].checked;
				}

				checkboxEls.forEach((cEl, index) => {

					if (cEl.checked) {
						result += popupSettings[id].options[index];

						if (index < popupSettings[id].options.length - 1) {
							result += ', ';
						}
					}
				});
            }

			result = result.trim();

			if (result.endsWith(',')) {
				result = result.substring(0, result.length - 1);
			}

            return result;
        }

        // get popup form values

        const getDate = () => {
            if (hasDateInput) {
                const dayInputEl = document.getElementById("mkt_popup_birthday_day");
                const yearInputEl = document.getElementById("mkt_popup_birthday_year");
                const monthInputEl = document.getElementById("mkt_popup_birthday_month");

                if (dayInputEl && yearInputEl && monthInputEl) {
                    return dayInputEl.value && monthInputEl.value && yearInputEl.value ? `${yearInputEl.value}-${monthInputEl.value}-${dayInputEl.value}` : null;
                }
            } else {
                return null;
            }
        }

        const getInputValue = (field) => {
            const inputEl = document.getElementById(`mkt_popup_subscriber_${field}`);

            if (inputEl) {
                return inputEl.value ? inputEl.value : null;
            }
        }

        const getDiscountCode = async (domainKey, email, rewardId) => {
            await fetch(`https://${clusterUrl}.themarketer.com/p/dc`, {
				method: 'POST',
				headers: {
					'Content-Type': 'application/json'
				},
				body: JSON.stringify({
					k: domainKey,
					email: email,
                    session: sessionStorage.getItem('mktr_popups_session_id'),
                    rId: rewardId,
                    pId: popupId
				})
			})
                .then(function (response) {
                    return response.json()
                }).then(function (res) {
                    discountCode = res.code;
                });
        }

        // subscribe

        const incrementSubscriberCount = async (params, domainKey) => {
			const displayToSubscribed = window.mktr_popups_data[popupId].rules.display_to_subscribed.on && templateType !== 'gamified';
            let isSubscribed = false;

            if (window.mktr_popups_user_data && Object.prototype.hasOwnProperty.call(window.mktr_popups_user_data, 'subscribed') && window.mktr_popups_user_data.subscribed && !displayToSubscribed) {
				isSubscribed = true;
                const alreadySubscribedEl = document.getElementById('mkt-content-input-exists-email');

                if (alreadySubscribedEl) {
                    alreadySubscribedEl.style.display = 'block';
                }
                return;

            }

            await fetch(`https://${clusterUrl}.themarketer.com/p/c?k=${domainKey}&email=${params.email}`).then(function (response) {
                return response.json()
            }).then(function (response) {
                if (Object.prototype.hasOwnProperty.call(response, 'subscribed')) {

                    if (response.subscribed === true || response.subscribed === 'true') {
                        isSubscribed = true;

						if (isSubscribed && !displayToSubscribed) {
						   const alreadySubscribedEl = document.getElementById('mkt-content-input-exists-email');

						   if (alreadySubscribedEl) {
							   alreadySubscribedEl.style.display = 'block';
						   }

						   if (subscribeButton) {
							   subscribeButton.disabled = false;
						   }
                       }
                    }
                }

                return;
            });

			if ((isSubscribed && displayToSubscribed) || !isSubscribed) {
                if (templateType === 'gamified') {
                    if (subscribeButton) {
                        subscribeButton.classList.add('button-loading');
                        subscribeButtonInnerHtml = subscribeButton.innerHTML;
                        subscribeButton.innerHTML = `<span class="mkt-popup-subscribe-button-loading"></span>`;
                    }
                }

                window.dataLayer.push({
                    event: "__sm__set_email",
                    email_address: params.email,
                    firstname: params.firstName,
                    lastname: params.lastName,
                    birthday: params.dateOfBirth,
                    phone: params.phone,
                    gender: params.gender,
                    source: 'popup',
                    tag: params.tag,
                    city: params.city,
                    custom_form_field_1: {
                        column: params.custom_form_field_1.column,
                        value: params.custom_form_field_1.value
                    },
                    custom_form_field_2: {
                        column: params.custom_form_field_2.column,
                        value: params.custom_form_field_2.value
                    },
                    custom_form_field_3: {
                        column: params.custom_form_field_3.column,
                        value: params.custom_form_field_3.value
                    },
                });

                if (templateType === 'gamified' && game === 'wof') {

                    const wheelContainer = document.getElementById('mkt-popup-content-wof-container')

                    if (wheelContainer) {
                        wheelContainer.classList.add('spining');

                        playWheelSound();

                        if (wof.slice.discount_type === 'multi_use' && !wof.slice.losing) {
                            discountCode = wof.slice.discount_code;
                        } else {
                            if (!wof.slice.losing) {
                                await getDiscountCode(domainKey, params.email, wof.slice.id);
                            }
                        }
                    }
                }

                if (templateType === 'gamified' && game === 'saw') {
                    if (saw.reward.discount_type === 'multi_use') {
                        discountCode = saw.reward.discount_code;
                    } else {
                        await getDiscountCode(domainKey, params.email, saw.reward.id);
                    }
                }

                if (templateType === 'gamified' && game === 'cag' && selectedCagRewardId !== null) {
                    const rewardSuccessEl = document.getElementById('mkt-popup-success-content');

                    if (rewardSuccessEl) {
                        const rewardHeaderEl = rewardSuccessEl.querySelector('.mkt-popup-headline');

                        if (rewardHeaderEl) {
                            const wonReward = cag.rewards.find(reward => reward.id === selectedCagRewardId);

                            rewardHeaderEl.innerHTML = rewardHeaderEl.innerHTML.replace('reward_label', wonReward.label).replaceAll("{", '').replaceAll("}", '');
                        }
                    }

                    await getDiscountCode(domainKey, params.email, selectedCagRewardId);
                }

                fetch(`https://${clusterUrl}.themarketer.com/p/i?k=${domainKey}&email=${params.email}&fId=${popupId}`);

                if (popupSettings.display_success_popup) {
                    if (templateType === 'gamified' && game === 'wof') {
                        setTimeout(() => {
                            displaySuccessPopup();
                        }, 7000);
                    } else {
                        displaySuccessPopup();
                    }
                } else {

                    if (subscribeButton) {
                        subscribeButton.disabled = false;
                    }

                    if (popupSettings.subscribe_button.action === 'redirect' && ![null, 'null', ''].includes(popupSettings.subscribe_button.redirect_url)) {
                        document.getElementById('theMarketer-popup-backdrop').remove();
                        window.location = popupSettings.subscribe_button.redirect_url;
                    } else {
                        document.getElementById('theMarketer-popup-backdrop').remove();
                    }
                }
			}
        }

        const displaySuccessPopup = () => {
            const popupContent = document.getElementById('mkt-popup-content');
            const popupImage = document.getElementById('mkt-popup-content-image');
            const popupSuccessContent = document.getElementById(popupSettings.layout === 'floating' && popupSettings.device === 'desktop' ? 'mkt-popup-floating-success-content' : 'mkt-popup-success-content');
            const popupSuccessImage = document.getElementById('mkt-popup-content-success-image');
            const successButtonEl = document.getElementById('mkt-popup-success-button');
            const popupWrapper = document.getElementById('mkt-popup-content-wrapper');
            const mainWrapper = document.getElementById('mkt-popup-wrapper');

            if (mainWrapper) {
                mainWrapper.classList.add('success');
            }

            popupContent.style.display = 'none';

            if (popupWrapper) {
                popupWrapper.classList.add('success');
            }

            if (popupSuccessContent) {
                popupSuccessContent.style.display = 'flex';
            }

            if (popupImage) {
                popupImage.style.display = 'none';
            }

            if (popupSuccessImage) {
                popupSuccessImage.style.display = 'flex';
            }

            if (templateType === 'gamified') {
                if (!wof.slice.losing) {
                    successButtonEl.textContent = discountCode;
                }

                if (game === 'cag') {
                    const chosenSuccessGiftEl = document.getElementById(`success-gift-${selectedCagRewardId}`);

                    if (chosenSuccessGiftEl) {
                        chosenSuccessGiftEl.classList.add('chosen');
                    }
                }
            }

            if (subscribeButton) {
                subscribeButton.disabled = false;

                if (templateType === 'gamified') {
                    subscribeButton.innerHTML = subscribeButtonInnerHtml;
                    subscribeButton.classList.remove('button-loading');
                }
            }

            setTimeout(() => {
                successButtonEl.addEventListener('click', () => {
                    if (templateType === 'gamified') {
                        if (!discountCodeCopied && !wof.slice.losing) {
                            copyToClipboard(successButtonEl.textContent);

                            successButtonEl.innerHTML = successButtonEl.textContent + ' &#x2713;';

                            discountCodeCopied = true;
                        }

                        if (wof.slice.losing) {
                            document.getElementById('theMarketer-popup-backdrop').remove();
                        }
                    } else {
                        if (popupSettings.success_button.action === 'redirect' && popupSettings.success_button.redirect_url !== null) {
                            window.location = popupSettings.success_button.redirect_url;
                        } else {
                            document.getElementById('theMarketer-popup-backdrop').remove();
                        }
                    }
                });
            }, 200);
        }

        function getCookie() {
            const value = `; ${document.cookie}`;
            const parts = value.split(`; __sm__c=`);

			if (parts.length >= 2) {
				return parts[1].split(';').shift();
			}
        }

        const copyToClipboard = (text) => {
            navigator.clipboard.writeText(text);
        }

        const addSubscriber = (params) => {
            const data = {...params};

            const mktCookie = JSON.parse(getCookie() || '{}');

            if (data.name !== null && data.name !== undefined) {

                const trimmedName = data.name.trim();
                const firstWhiteSpaceIndex = trimmedName.indexOf(' ');

                if (firstWhiteSpaceIndex > -1) {
                    data.firstName = trimmedName.substring(0, firstWhiteSpaceIndex);
                    data.lastName = trimmedName.substring(firstWhiteSpaceIndex + 1);
                } else {
                    data.firstName = trimmedName;
                    data.lastName = null;
                }

            } else {
                data.firstname = data.firstName ? data.firstName : null;
                data.lastname = data.lastName ? data.lastName : null;
            }

            subscribeButton.disabled = true;

            incrementSubscriberCount(data, mktCookie.k);
        }

        const spinSound = new Audio("https://cdn1.mktr2.com/signup-forms/popups/assets/wof/sounds/basic.mp3");

        const playWheelSound = () => {
            if (popupSettings.wheel_settings.wheel_sound) {
                spinSound.play();
            }
        }

        const subscribeButton = document.getElementById('mkt-popup-subscribe-button');

        if (subscribeButton) {
            if (['saw', 'cag'].includes(game) && !subscribeButton.classList.contains('disabled') && !preview) {
                subscribeButton.classList.add('disabled');
                subscribeButton.disabled = true;
            }

            const params = {
                dateOfBirth: null,
                email: null,
                name: null,
                firstName: null,
                lastName: null,
                phone: null,
                gender: null,
                privacyPolicy: false,
                tag: null,
                custom_form_field_1: {
                    column: popupSettings['custom_form_field_1'].hide ? null : popupSettings['custom_form_field_1']?.column_name,
                    value: null
                },
                custom_form_field_2: {
                    column: popupSettings['custom_form_field_2'].hide ? null : popupSettings['custom_form_field_2']?.column_name,
                    value: null
                },
                custom_form_field_3: {
                    column: popupSettings['custom_form_field_3'].hide ? null : popupSettings['custom_form_field_3']?.column_name,
                    value: null
                }
            }

            subscribeButton.addEventListener('click', function (e) {

                if (!sawAreaTouched && game === 'saw') {
                    return;
                }

                let emptyRequiredInputField = false;
                params.email = getInputValue('email');

                if (!popupSettings['email_input']['hide']) {

                    if (!document.getElementById('mkt_popup_subscriber_email')) {
                        document.getElementById('theMarketer-popup-backdrop').remove();

                        return;
                    }

                    if (params.email === null) {
                        emailRequiredEl.style.display = 'block';
                        return;
                    }

                    if (!checkEmailFormat(params.email)) {
                        return;
                    }
                }

                params.name = getInputValue('name');
                params.firstName = getInputValue('first_name');
                params.lastName = getInputValue('last_name');
                params.phone = getInputValue('phone');
                params.dateOfBirth = getDate();
                params.gender = getGender();
                params.privacyPolicy = getPrivacyPolicy();

                ['custom_form_field_1', 'custom_form_field_2', 'custom_form_field_3'].forEach(csField => {
                    if (!popupSettings[csField].hide) {

                        if (params[csField].column !== '' && params[csField].column !== null && params[csField].column !== undefined) {

                            if (['First name', 'Last name', 'City'].includes(params[csField].column)) {
                                params[baseColumns[params[csField].column]] = getCustomFieldInputValue(csField);
                            } else {
                                params[csField].value = getCustomFieldInputValue(csField);
                            }

                        }
                    }
                });

                if (nameInputEl && params.name === null && popupSettings['name_input']['required']) {
                    nameErrorEl.style.display = 'block';
                    emptyRequiredInputField = true;
                }

                if (firstNameInputEl && params.firstName === null && popupSettings['first_name']['required']) {
                    firstNameErrorEl.style.display = 'block';
                    emptyRequiredInputField = true;
                }

                if (lastNameInputEl && params.lastName === null && popupSettings['last_name']['required']) {
                    lastNameErrorEl.style.display = 'block';
                    emptyRequiredInputField = true;
                }

                if (phoneInputEl && params.phone === null && popupSettings['phone_input']['required']) {
                    phoneErrorEl.style.display = 'block';
                    emptyRequiredInputField = true;
                }

                if (hasDateInput && params.dateOfBirth === null && popupSettings['date_of_birth']['required']) {
                    dateErrorEl.style.display = 'block';
                    emptyRequiredInputField = true;
                }

                if (genderInputEl && params.gender === null && popupSettings['gender_select']['required']) {
                    genderErrorEl.style.display = 'block';
                    emptyRequiredInputField = true;
                }

                if (genderInputEl) {
                    params.gender = genderInputEl.selectedIndex === 1 ? 'M' : genderInputEl.selectedIndex === 2 ? 'F' : 'U';
                }

                if (privacyPolicyEl && params.privacyPolicy === false && popupSettings['privacy_policy']['required']) {
                    privacyPolicyErrorEl.style.display = 'block';
                    emptyRequiredInputField = true;
                }

                ['custom_form_field_1', 'custom_form_field_2', 'custom_form_field_3'].forEach(field => {
                    if (customFields[field].el && popupSettings[field]['required'] && popupSettings[field]['type'] !== 'checkbox') {
                        if (popupSettings[field]['type'] === 'select' && customFields[field].el.selectedIndex === 0) {
                            customFields[field].error.style.display = 'block';
                            emptyRequiredInputField = true;
                        }

                        if (popupSettings[field]['type'] === 'input' && (customFields[field].el.value === '' || customFields[field].el.value === null)) {
                            customFields[field].error.style.display = 'block';
                            emptyRequiredInputField = true;
                        }
                    }
                });

                if (emptyRequiredInputField || wrongEmailFormat) {
                    return;
                }

                if (popupSettings['subscription_options']['tag_contacts']) {
                    if (typeof popupSettings['subscription_options']['tag'] === 'object' && popupSettings['subscription_options']['tag'] !== null) {
                       params.tag = popupSettings['subscription_options']['tag']?.value;
                    } else {
                        params.tag = popupSettings['subscription_options']['tag'];
                    }
                }

                if (popupSettings['email_input']['hide'] && (templateType !== 'gamified' && game !== 'wof')) {
                    displaySuccessPopup();
                }

                addSubscriber(params);

            });
        }

        if (game === 'saw') {
            function applyStyle(ctx, style) {
Object.keys(style).forEach(key => ctx[key] = style[key])
}

function ease(val, power) {
return val < 0 ? 0 : val > 1 ? 1 : Math.pow(val, power)
}

const settings = {
width: 240,
height: 120,
coveragedMin: 0.3,
coverColor: popupSettings.saw_settings.background,
mouseEvents: ['mouseup', 'mousedown', 'mousemove', 'touchstart', 'touchend', 'touchmove'],
coverImage: loadImage(popupSettings.saw_settings.pattern),
container: document.getElementById('mkt-popup-content-scratch'),
drawStyle: {
radius: 20,
shadowBlur: 15,
shadowOffsetX: 0,
shadowOffsetY: 0,
shadowColor: popupSettings.saw_settings.background,
fillStyle: popupSettings.saw_settings.background,
globalCompositeOperation: "destination-out",
},
coverageArray: (() => {
const buf = new Uint8Array(64);
buf.fill(1);
return buf
})(),
}

let update = true;
const mouse = {x: 0, y: 0, button: false};

function mouseEvent(e) {
const canvasRect = settings.container.getBoundingClientRect();

if (mobileCheck() && e.touches && e.touches[0]) {
mouse.x = e.touches[0].pageX - canvasRect.left - scrollX;
mouse.y = e.touches[0].pageY - canvasRect.top - scrollY;
} else {
mouse.x = e.pageX - canvasRect.left - scrollX;
mouse.y = e.pageY - canvasRect.top - scrollY;
}

if (['mousedown', 'touchstart'].includes(e.type)) {
mouse.button = true;
} else if (['mouseup', 'touchend'].includes(e.type)) {
mouse.button = false;
}

update = true;
}

function fillCircle(ctx, x, y, style) {
applyStyle(ctx, style);
ctx.beginPath();
ctx.arc(x, y, style.radius, 0, Math.PI * 2);
ctx.fill();
}

function setCoverage(array, x, y) {
let i = array.length - 1;
const size = Math.sqrt(array.length) | 0;
array[(x * size) | ((y * size) | 0) * size] = 0;
let count = 0;

while (i-- > 0) {
count += array[i]
}

return count / array.length;
}

function loadImage(url) {
const image = new Image();
image.src = url;
image.rendered = false;

const prizeEl = document.getElementById('mkt-popup-content-scratch-result');

if (prizeEl) {
prizeEl.classList.add('visible');
}

return image;
}

function createCanvas(width, height) {
const canvas = document.getElementById('mkt-popup-content-scratch-canvas');
canvas.width = width;
canvas.height = height;
canvas.ctx = canvas.getContext("2d");
return canvas;
}

(function (settings) {
const canvas = createCanvas(settings.width, settings.height);
const ctx = canvas.ctx;
settings.mouseEvents.forEach(eventName => addEventListener(eventName, mouseEvent));
let reveal = false;
let fade = 1;
ctx.fillStyle = settings.coverColor;
ctx.fillRect(0, 0, canvas.width, canvas.height);

(function mainLoop() {
if (settings.coverImage.complete && !settings.coverImage.rendered) {
ctx.globalCompositeOperation = "source-over";
ctx.drawImage(settings.coverImage, 0, 0, settings.width, settings.height);
settings.coverImage.rendered = true;
const swipeEl = document.getElementById("mkt-popup-content-scratch-canvas");
swipeEl.className = "swipe-area loaded";
}
if (update) {  // only if needed render canvas
if (settings.coverImage.rendered) {
mouse.button && fillCircle(ctx, mouse.x, mouse.y, settings.drawStyle);
setCoverage(settings.coverageArray, mouse.x / settings.width, mouse.y / settings.height) < settings.coveragedMin && (reveal = true);
update = false;
}
if (reveal) {
fade -= 0.05;
canvas.style.opacity = ease(fade, 2);
update = true;
}
}
if (reveal && fade <= 0) {
const swipeEl = document.getElementById("mkt-popup-content-scratch-canvas");
swipeEl.style.cursor = "pointer";
settings.container.removeChild(canvas);
settings.mouseEvents.forEach(eventName => removeEventListener(eventName, mouseEvent));

sawAreaTouched = true;

if (subscribeButton && subscribeButton.classList.contains('disabled')) {
subscribeButton.classList.remove('disabled');
subscribeButton.disabled = false;
}

} else {
requestAnimationFrame(mainLoop);
}
}());
}(settings));        }

        if (game === 'cag') {
            if (cag?.rewards?.length) {
cag.rewards.forEach(reward => {
const rewardEl = document.getElementById(reward.id);

if (rewardEl) {
rewardEl.addEventListener('click', () => {
if (selectedCagRewardId === null) {
selectedCagRewardId = rewardEl.id;

const chosenGiftEl = document.getElementById(`chosen-gift-${rewardEl.id}`);

rewardEl.classList.add('checked');

if (chosenGiftEl) {
chosenGiftEl.classList.add('selected');
}

subscribeButton && subscribeButton.classList.remove('disabled');
subscribeButton.disabled = false;
}
});
}
});
}
        }

    })();

</script></head>

			function _addCss(url, attribute, value, loaded){
				var _s = document.createElement('link');
				_s.rel = 'stylesheet';
				_s.href = url;
				_s.type = 'text/css';
				if(attribute)
				{
					_s.setAttribute(attribute, value)
				}
				if(loaded){
					_s.onload = function(){
						var dom = document.getElementsByTagName('body')[0];
						//dom.classList.remove('loading');
					}
				}
				var _st = document.getElementsByTagName('link')[0];
				_st.parentNode.insertBefore(_s, _st);
			}

<div id="_cartSummary" class="hide"></div>

<script>
	$(document).ready(function() {

		$(document).on('keypress', '.-g-input-loader', function(){
			$(this).addClass('-g-input-loading');
		})

		$.Gomag.bind('Product/Add/To/Cart/After', function(eventResponse, properties)
		{
									var data = JSON.parse(properties.data);
			$('.q-cart').html(data.quantity);
			if(parseFloat(data.quantity) > 0)
			{
				$('.q-cart').removeClass('hide');
			}
			else
			{
				$('.q-cart').addClass('hide');
			}
			$('.cartPrice').html(data.subtotal + ' ' + data.currency);
			$('.cartProductCount').html(data.quantity);


		})
		$('#_cartSummary').on('updateCart', function(event, cart) {
			var t = $(this);

			$.get('https://www.lexshop.ro/cart-update', {
				cart: cart
			}, function(data) {

				$('.q-cart').html(data.quantity);
				if(parseFloat(data.quantity) > 0)
				{
					$('.q-cart').removeClass('hide');
				}
				else
				{
					$('.q-cart').addClass('hide');
				}
				$('.cartPrice').html(data.subtotal + ' ' + data.currency);
				$('.cartProductCount').html(data.quantity);
			}, 'json');
			window.ga = window.ga || function() {
				(ga.q = ga.q || []).push(arguments)
			};
			ga('send', 'event', 'Buton', 'Click', 'Adauga_Cos');
		});

		if(window.gtag_report_conversion) {
			$(document).on("click", 'li.phone-m', function() {
				var phoneNo = $('li.phone-m').children( "a").attr('href');
				gtag_report_conversion(phoneNo);
			});

		}

	});
</script>

				<script>
			$(document).ready(function() {

				$('#_autocompleteSearchMainHeader').autocomplete({
					serviceUrl: 'https://www.lexshop.ro/autocomplete',
					minChars: 2,
					deferRequestBy: 700,
					appendTo: '#_searchFormMainHeader',
					width: parseInt($('#_doSearch').offset().left) - parseInt($('#_autocompleteSearchMainHeader').offset().left),
					formatResult: function(suggestion, currentValue) {
						return suggestion.value;
					},
					onSelect: function(suggestion) {
						$(this).val(suggestion.data);
					},
					onSearchComplete: function(suggestion) {
						$(this).removeClass('-g-input-loading');
						$.Gomag.trigger('Autocomplete/Search/Complete', {search:$('#_autocompleteSearchMainHeader').val()});
					}
				});
				$(document).on('click', '#_doSearch', function(e){
					e.preventDefault();
					if($('#_autocompleteSearchMainHeader').val() != '')
					{
						$('#_searchFormMainHeader').submit();
					}
				})
			});
		</script>

		<form name="search-form" class="search-form" action="https://www.lexshop.ro/produse" id="_searchFormMobileToggle">
			<input id="_autocompleteSearchMobileToggle" name="c" class="input-placeholder -g-input-loader" type="text" autofocus="autofocus" value="" placeholder="Cauta in site..." aria-label="Search" autocomplete="off">
			<button id="_doSearchMobile" class="search-button" aria-hidden="true">
				<i class="fa fa-search" aria-hidden="true"></i>
			</button>

										<script>
					$(document).ready(function() {
						$('#_autocompleteSearchMobileToggle').autocomplete({
							serviceUrl: 'https://www.lexshop.ro/autocomplete',
							minChars: 2,
							deferRequestBy: 700,
							appendTo: '#_searchFormMobileToggle',
							width: parseInt($('#_doSearchMobile').offset().left) - parseInt($('#_autocompleteSearchMobileToggle').offset().left),
							formatResult: function(suggestion, currentValue) {
								return suggestion.value;
							},
							onSelect: function(suggestion) {
								$(this).val(suggestion.data);
							},
							onSearchComplete: function(suggestion) {
								$(this).removeClass('-g-input-loading');
								$.Gomag.trigger('Autocomplete/Search/Complete', {search:$('#_autocompleteSearchMobileToggle').val()});
							}
						});

						$(document).on('click', '#_doSearchMobile', function(e){
							e.preventDefault();
							if($('#_autocompleteSearchMobileToggle').val() != '')
							{
								$('#_searchFormMobileToggle').submit();
							}
						})
					});
				</script>
			
		<div class="autocomplete-suggestions" style="position: absolute; display: none; width: 0px; max-height: 300px; z-index: 9999;"></div></form>

<script>
	$(document).ready(function(){
		$('#_subscribe').on('click', function(e){
			e.preventDefault();
			$('#_emailAddress').attr('name', 'email');
			

			$.post('https://www.lexshop.ro/abonare-newsletter', $('#main-newsletter-form').serializeArray(), function(data){
				var result = data.result;

				var p = 'error';

				if(result == 1) {
					p = 'succes';
				} else if(result == 11) {
					p = 'succesOptIn';
				} else if(result == 2) {
					p = 'mail_exists';
				} else if(result == -1) {
					p = 'mail_exists';
				} else if(result == 'noUserAgreement') {
					p = 'noUserAgreement';
				}
				if(p == 'succes' || p == 'succesOptIn' || p == 'mail_exists')
				{
					var values ={email:$('#_emailAddress').val()};
					$.Gomag.trigger('INFO_USER',{data:values});

					$('#_emailAddress').val('');
										$('.-g-agreement-NewsletterInformation').find('input[name="agreeNewsletterInformation"]').attr('checked', false);
				}
				if((p == 'succes' || p == 'succesOptIn' || p == 'mail_exists') && $.Gomag.getWidgets('popup:newletterSubscriptionConfirm') !== false)
				{
					$.Gomag.triggerPopup('popup:newletterSubscriptionConfirm');
				}
				else
				{
					$.Gomag.openDefaultPopup(undefined, {
						src : 'https://www.lexshop.ro/iframe-newsletter?p='+p,
						iframe : {css : {width : '400px'}}
					});
				}
			}, "json");
		});
	});
</script>

	$.Gomag.bind('Product/Box/Click', function enhancedAnalyticsV4(queue){
		$.Gomag.asyncClickBlock(queue);
		if(
			typeof(gaProducts) != 'undefined'
			&& 
			gaProducts[queue.data.product] != undefined
		)
		{
			var clickProduct = gaProducts[queue.data.product];
		}
		else
		{
			var clickProduct = {};
			var productId = queue.data.product;
			
			var envData = $.Gomag.getEnvData();
			var products = envData.products;
	
			if(products[productId] !== undefined){

				var dataProduct = products[productId];
				
				clickProduct.item_id = dataProduct.id ;
				clickProduct.item_name =  dataProduct.name ;
				clickProduct.item_brand = dataProduct.brand;
				clickProduct.item_category = dataProduct.category;
				clickProduct.item_vat = dataProduct.vat;
				clickProduct.price = parseFloat(dataProduct.price).toFixed(2);
				clickProduct.quantity = 1;
				
			}
		}
		
		gtag("event", "select_item", {
		  items: [clickProduct]
		});
		setTimeout(function(){ $.Gomag.asyncClickComplete(queue);}, 200);
	});

    $(document).ready(function () {
        $.Gomag.bind('Product/Sort/Before/Redirect', function productFilterSendData(event, data) {
            if (data && data.sort && data.sort.options && data.sort.selectedIndex !== undefined) {
                var selectedOption = data.sort.options[data.sort.selectedIndex];

                if (selectedOption) {
                    var orderType = $(selectedOption).data('sorttype') || 'unknown';

                    window.dataLayer = window.dataLayer || [];
                    window.dataLayer.push({
                        'event': 'product_sort',
                        'sort_option': orderType
                    });
                }
            }
        });
    });
</script>
<script>
	function processFilterGroupSelected(parent, removeValue = undefined) {
        let eventData = { event: 'product_filter' };

		if (removeValue === 'all') {
			eventData.remove_value = removeValue;
		} else {
			$(parent).find('.filter.box').each(function(){
				let filterKey = $(this).attr('data-filterkey');
				if (filterKey) {

					let filterValues = [];

					$(this).find('a.active-account').each(function(){
						filterValues.push($(this).text().trim());
					});


					$(this).find('.checked').each(function(){
						let linkedText = $(this).parent().find('a').data('filtervalue');
						if ((linkedText && removeValue === undefined )|| (linkedText && removeValue != undefined && removeValue != linkedText) ) {
							filterValues.push(linkedText);
						}
					});


					if (filterValues.length > 0) {
						eventData[filterKey] = filterValues;
					};
				};
			});
		}


		if ($('#orderType').length > 0) {
			let orderType = $('#orderType option:selected').data('sorttype');
			eventData.sort_option = orderType;
		}

		windowsdataLayer = window.dataLayer || [];
		windowsdataLayer.push(eventData);
    }
	$.Gomag.bind('Product/Filter/Before/Redirect', function productFilterSendData(event, data){

		});

	$.Gomag.bind('Product/Box/Click', function enhancedAnalyticsV4(queue){
		$.Gomag.asyncClickBlock(queue);
		if(
			typeof(gaProducts) != 'undefined'
			&& 
			gaProducts[queue.data.product] != undefined
		)
		{
			var clickProduct = gaProducts[queue.data.product];
		}
		else
		{
			var clickProduct = {};
			var productId = queue.data.product;
			
			var envData = $.Gomag.getEnvData();
			var products = envData.products;
	
			if(products[productId] !== undefined){

				var dataProduct = products[productId];
				
				clickProduct.item_id =dataProduct.id;
				clickProduct.item_name = dataProduct.sku;
				clickProduct.item_brand = dataProduct.brand;
				clickProduct.item_category = dataProduct.category;
				clickProduct.price = parseFloat(dataProduct.price).toFixed(2);
				clickProduct.item_vat = dataProduct.vat;
				clickProduct.quantity = 1;
				
			}
		}
		
		gtag("event", "select_item", {
			send_to: 'gomag',
		  items: [clickProduct]
		});
		setTimeout(function(){ $.Gomag.asyncClickComplete(queue);}, 200);
	});

    $(document).ready(function () {
        $.Gomag.bind('Product/Sort/Before/Redirect', function productFilterSendDataAQ(event, data) {
            if (data && data.sort && data.sort.options && data.sort.selectedIndex !== undefined) {
                var selectedOption = data.sort.options[data.sort.selectedIndex];

                if (selectedOption) {
                    var orderType = $(selectedOption).data('sorttype') || 'unknown';

                    dataLayerAq = window.dataLayerAq || [];
                    dataLayerAq.push({
                        'event': 'product_sort',
                        'sort_option': orderType
                    });
                }
            }
        });
    });
</script>
<script>
	function processFilterGroupSelectedAq(parent, removeValue = undefined) {
        let eventData = { event: 'product_filter' };

		if (removeValue === 'all') {
			eventData.remove_value = removeValue;
		} else {
			$(parent).find('.filter.box').each(function(){
				let filterKey = $(this).attr('data-filterkey');
				if (filterKey) {

					let filterValues = [];

					$(this).find('a.active-account').each(function(){
						filterValues.push($(this).text().trim());
					});


					$(this).find('.checked').each(function(){
						let linkedText = $(this).parent().find('a').data('filtervalue');
						if ((linkedText && removeValue === undefined )|| (linkedText && removeValue != undefined && removeValue != linkedText) ) {
							filterValues.push(linkedText);
						}
					});


					if (filterValues.length > 0) {
						eventData[filterKey] = filterValues;
					};
				};
			});
		}


		if ($('#orderType').length > 0) {
			let orderType = $('#orderType option:selected').data('sorttype');
			eventData.sort_option = orderType;
		}

		dataLayerAq = window.dataLayerAq || [];
		dataLayerAq.push(eventData);
    }
	$.Gomag.bind('Product/Filter/Before/Redirect', function productFilterSendData(event, data){
			processFilterGroupSelectedAq(data.parent);
		});

	$(document).on('click', '.filter-remove', function (e) {
		let parent = $('#nav-filter');
		let removeValue = ($(this).data('deletefiltervalue') || "").toString().trim();
        processFilterGroupSelectedAq(parent, removeValue);
    });
	$(document).on('click', '.-g-category-filter-remove', function (e) {
		let parent = $('#nav-filter');
        processFilterGroupSelectedAq(parent, 'all');
    });

</script><script>

	$.Gomag.bind('User/Ajax/Data/Loaded', function productListDataValues(event, data){

		var categoryProducts = {"28764":28764,"11509":11509,"28761":28761,"15897":15897};

		if(categoryProducts.length == 0 || categoryProducts == undefined || categoryProducts == null) {
			return false;
		}

		if(data.data.stockAlertProducts !== undefined) {
			$.each(data.data.stockAlertProducts, function(i, v){
				$.each(categoryProducts, function (j, elem) {
					if(v == elem) {
						$('#stockAlertBTN'+v).find('i').removeClass('fa-bell-o').addClass('fa-check');
						$('#stockAlertBTN'+v).prop("onclick", null).off("click");
					}
				});
			});
		}

	})
</script>

<script>
	$.Gomag.bind('Product/Add/To/Cart/After', function(eventResponse, properties)
	{
		if(properties.product == undefined)
		{
			return false;
		}
		var product = properties.product;

		fbq('track', 'AddToCart', {
			content_name: product.name,
    		content_category: product.category,
    		content_ids: [product.sku],
    		content_type: 'product',
    		value: parseFloat(product.price).toFixed(2),
    		currency: String(product.currency).toLowerCase() == 'lei' ? 'RON' : product.currency
		});
	});
</script>
<script>
	$.Gomag.bind('Product/Add/To/Wishlist/After', function(eventResponse, properties)
	{

		if(properties.product == undefined)
		{
			return false;
		}
		var product = properties.product;
		fbq('track', 'AddToWishlist', {

    		content_category: product.category,
    		content_ids: [product.sku],
    		content_type: 'product',
    		value: parseFloat(product.price).toFixed(2),
    		currency: String(product.currency).toLowerCase() == 'lei' ? 'RON' : product.currency
		});
	});

	$(document).ready(function() {
		$('li.contact-header > a[href^="tel:"]').on('click', function() {
			let loggedStatus = 'guest';
			if($.Gomag.loggedInCustomer != undefined && ($.Gomag.loggedInCustomer.email != undefined && $.Gomag.loggedInCustomer.email != '') ||  ($.Gomag.loggedInCustomer.phone != undefined && $.Gomag.loggedInCustomer.phone != ''))
			{
				loggedStatus = '‘logged’';
			}
			windowsdataLayer = window.dataLayer || [];
			windowsdataLayer.push({
				'event': 'contact_call',
				'loggedStatus': loggedStatus
			});
		});
	});
	$.Gomag.bind('Product/Add/To/Wishlist/After', function addToWishlistLoadDataLayerTagManager(event, data){
		if(data.product !== undefined && data.data.action == 'add'){
            windowsdataLayer = window.dataLayer || [];
            windowsdataLayer.push({ ecommerce: null });
            windowsdataLayer.push({
                    event: "add_to_wishlist",
                    ecommerce: {
                        currency: data.product.currency,
                        value: data.product.price,
                        items: [{
                            item_id:  String(data.product.id) ,
                            item_name: data.product.name,
                            currency: data.product.currency,
                            discount: parseFloat(parseFloat(data.product.basePrice).toFixed(2) - parseFloat(data.product.price).toFixed(2)),
                            item_brand: data.product.brand,
                            item_category: data.product.category,
                            price: parseFloat(parseFloat(data.product.basePrice).toFixed(2)),
                            quantity: 1
                        }]
                    }
                });
        }
	})

    $.Gomag.bind('Product/Add/To/Cart/After', function addToCartLoadDataLayerTagManager(event, data){
		if(data.product !== undefined){

		var itemCategory = data.product.category;
		var itemCategory2 = '';
		var itemCategory3 = '';
		var itemCategory4 = '';
		var itemCategory5 = '';
		var itemDiscount = parseFloat(data.product.basePrice) > parseFloat(data.product.price) ? parseFloat(parseFloat(data.product.basePrice).toFixed(2) - parseFloat(data.product.price).toFixed(2)) : 0;

		if(typeof __productTagManagerInfoForAddToCart != 'undefined')
		{
			__productTagManagerInfoForAddToCart.forEach(function(e) {
				if (data.product.id == e.id)
				{
					itemCategory = e.item_category;
					itemCategory2 = e.item_category2;
					itemCategory3 = e.item_category3;
					itemCategory4 = e.item_category4;
					itemCategory5 = e.item_category5;
					itemDiscount = e.item_discount;
				}
			});
		}

		windowsdataLayer = window.dataLayer || [];
            windowsdataLayer.push({ ecommerce: null });
            windowsdataLayer.push({
                    event: "add_to_cart",
                    ecommerce: {
                        items: [{
                            item_id:  String(data.product.id) ,
                            item_name: data.product.name,
                            currency: String(data.product.currency).toLowerCase() == 'lei' ? 'RON' : data.product.currency,
                            discount: itemDiscount,
                            item_brand: data.product.brand ? data.product.brand : '',
                            item_category: itemCategory,
                            item_category2: itemCategory2,
                            item_category3: itemCategory3,
                            item_category4: itemCategory4,
                            item_category5: itemCategory5,
                            price: parseFloat(parseFloat(data.product.basePrice).toFixed(2)),
                            quantity: parseFloat(data.product.cartQuantity)
                        }]
                    }
            });

        }
	})

    $.Gomag.bind('Product/Remove/From/Cart', function deleteToCartLoadDataLayerTagManager(event, data){
        var envData = $.Gomag.getEnvData();

		if(data.data.product !== undefined && envData.products[data.data.product] !== undefined){
            var prod = envData.products[data.data.product];
            windowsdataLayer = window.dataLayer || [];
            windowsdataLayer.push({ ecommerce: null });
            windowsdataLayer.push({
                    event: "remove_from_cart",
                    ecommerce: {
                        items: [{
                            item_id:  String(prod.id) ,
                            item_name: prod.name,
                            currency: prod.currency,
                            discount: parseFloat(parseFloat(prod.basePrice).toFixed(2) - parseFloat(prod.price).toFixed(2)),
                            item_brand: prod.brand,
                            item_category: prod.category,
                            price: parseFloat(parseFloat(prod.basePrice).toFixed(2)),
                            quantity: data.data.quantity
                        }]
                    }
            });
        }
	})

    $.Gomag.bind('Cart/Quantity/Update', function updateCartLoadDataLayerTagManager(event, data){
        var envData = $.Gomag.getEnvData();

        if(parseFloat(data.data.initialQuantity) < parseFloat(data.data.finalQuantity)){

            if(data.data.product !== undefined && envData.products[data.data.product] !== undefined){
            var prod = envData.products[data.data.product];

            windowsdataLayer = window.dataLayer || [];
            windowsdataLayer.push({ ecommerce: null });
            windowsdataLayer.push({
                        event: "add_to_cart",
                        ecommerce: {
                            items: [{
                                item_id:  String(prod.id) ,
                                item_name: prod.name,
                                currency: String(prod.currency).toLowerCase() == 'lei' ? 'RON' : prod.currency,
                                discount: parseFloat(prod.basePrice) > parseFloat(prod.price) ? parseFloat(parseFloat(prod.basePrice) - parseFloat(prod.price)).toFixed(2) : 0,
                                item_brand: prod.brand ? prod.brand : '',
                                item_category: prod.category,
                                price: parseFloat(parseFloat(prod.basePrice).toFixed(2)),
                                quantity: 1
                            }]
                        }
                });

            }
        }
        else if(parseFloat(data.data.initialQuantity) > parseFloat(data.data.finalQuantity)){

            if(data.data.product !== undefined && envData.products[data.data.product] !== undefined){
                var prod = envData.products[data.data.product];
                windowsdataLayer = window.dataLayer || [];
                windowsdataLayer.push({ ecommerce: null });
                windowsdataLayer.push({
                        event: "remove_from_cart",
                        ecommerce: {
                            items: [{
                                item_id:  String(prod.id) ,
                                item_name: prod.name,
                                currency: prod.currency,
                                discount: parseFloat(parseFloat(parseFloat(prod.basePrice).toFixed(2)) - parseFloat(prod.price.toFixed(2))),

                                item_category: prod.category,
                                price: parseFloat(parseFloat(prod.basePrice).toFixed(2)),
                                quantity: 1
                            }]
                        }
                });
            }
        }


	})

	$.Gomag.bind('INFO_USER', function infoUserLoadEmailDataTheMarketer(event, data){
		if(data.data.email !== undefined) {
			if(data.data.lastname == undefined) {
				data.data.lastname = '';
			}

			if(data.data.firstname == undefined) {
				data.data.firstname = '';
			}

			if(data.data.phone !== undefined) {
				data.data.phone = '';
			}

			dataLayer.push({
				event: "__sm__set_email",
				email_address: data.data.email,
				firstname: data.data.firstname,
				lastname: data.data.lastname,
				phone: data.data.phone
			});
		}
	})

	$.Gomag.bind('Cart/Quantity/Update', function (event, data){
		if(!(document.cookie.match(/^(.*;)?\s*user\s*=\s*[^;]+(.*)?$/) || document.cookie.match(/^(.*;)?\s*_gs\s*=\s*[^;]+(.*)?$/))){
    
			var envData = $.Gomag.getEnvData();
			var products = envData.products;
			if(!data.data.finalQuantity || !data.data.initialQuantity)
			{
				return false;
			}
			var dataProduct = products[data.data.product];
			if(dataProduct == undefined)
			{
				return false;
			}
			
			if(parseFloat(data.data.initialQuantity) < parseFloat(data.data.finalQuantity))
			{
				var quantity = parseFloat(data.data.finalQuantity) - parseFloat(data.data.initialQuantity);
				
				va('ecom','add_to_cart',{ 
					"customer": { 
						"id": "0", 
						"name": "", 
						"email": "", 
						"phoneNumber": "" 
					}, 
					"currency": dataProduct.currency ? (String(dataProduct.currency).toLowerCase() == 'lei' ? 'RON' : dataProduct.currency) : 'RON', 
					"value":0.00, 
					"items":[ 
						{ "id": dataProduct.sku, 
							"item_name": dataProduct.name, 
							"affiliation": "", 
							"coupon": "", 
							"discount": 0, 
							"index": 0, 
							"item_brand": dataProduct.brand, 
							"item_category": dataProduct.category, 
							"item_list_id": "", 
							"item_list_name": "", 
							"item_variant": "", 
							"location_id": "", 
							"price": dataProduct.price, 
							"quantity": quantity, 
							"image_url": dataProduct.image
						} 
					] 
				})
			}
			else if(parseFloat(data.data.initialQuantity) > parseFloat(data.data.finalQuantity))
			{
				var quantity = parseFloat(data.data.initialQuantity) - parseFloat(data.data.finalQuantity);
				
				va('ecom','remove_from_cart',{ 
					"customer": { 
						"id": "0", 
						"name": "", 
						"email": "",

            dataLayerAq.push({
                    event: "add_to_wishlist",

                        currency: data.product.currency,
                        value: data.product.price,
                        items: [{
                            item_id: String(data.product.id),

    $.Gomag.bind('Product/Add/To/Cart/After', function addToCartLoadDataLayerAqurate(event, data){
		if(data.product !== undefined){

		var itemCategory = data.product.category;

					itemCategory3 = e.item_category3;
					itemCategory4 = e.item_category4;
					itemCategory5 = e.item_category5;
					itemDiscount = e.item_discount;
				}
			});
		}

            dataLayerAq.push({ ecommerce: null });
            dataLayerAq.push({
                    event: "add_to_cart",
                    ecommerce: {

                            item_id: String(data.product.id),
